             '            GROUP BY trade_id\n'
             '        ) r ON t.trade_id = r.trade_id\n'
             '        LEFT JOIN portfolio_managers pm ON s.manager_id = pm.manager_id\n'
             "        WHERE t.trade_date BETWEEN '2023-01-01' AND '2023-12-31'\n"
             '        AND s.sharpe_ratio > 1.5\n'
             '        ORDER BY t.trade_date DESC;\n'

### SQL Query Optimization for Olivia:
To optimize Olivia's query, here are the suggested approaches:
1. **Index Suggestions**:
   - Add a **composite index** on frequently joined and filtered columns:
     - `trades.trade_date`, `trades.trade_id`.
     - `positions.trade_id`, `positions.strategy_id`.
     - `risk_calculations.trade_id`.

2. **Query Structure Tweaks**:
   - Use **CTEs (Common Table Expressions)** for legibility and modular optimization.
   - Avoid calculating aggregated risk metrics for all trades upfront—limit this to trades meeting the date/sharpe ratio conditions.

3. **SQL Rewrite**:
```sql
WITH FilteredTrades AS (
    SELECT t.trade_id, t.symbol, t.trade_date
    FROM trades t
    WHERE t.trade_date BETWEEN '2023-01-01' AND '2023-12-31'
),
FilteredStrategies AS (
    SELECT s.strategy_id, s.manager_id, s.sharpe_ratio, s.strategy_name
    FROM strategies s
    WHERE s.sharpe_ratio > 1.5
),
AggregatedRisk AS (
    SELECT trade_id, STRING_AGG(CONCAT(metric_name, ': ', value), '; ') as risk_metrics
    FROM risk_calculations
    GROUP BY trade_id
)
SELECT ft.trade_id, ft.symbol, p.position_size, fs.strategy_name, 
       ar.risk_metrics, pm.name as portfolio_manager
FROM FilteredTrades ft
LEFT JOIN positions p ON ft.trade_id = p.trade_id
LEFT JOIN FilteredStrategies fs ON p.strategy_id = fs.strategy_id
LEFT JOIN AggregatedRisk ar ON ft.trade_id = ar.trade_id
LEFT JOIN portfolio_managers pm ON fs.manager_id = pm.manager_id
ORDER BY ft.trade_date DESC;
```

This approach:
- Filters `trades` and `strategies` early to reduce dataset size.
- Uses `STRING_AGG` only for filtered trades.
- Modularizes with CTEs for clarity and maintainability.
